=============================
HVL: HVLvlo = 0 - 20
     HVL_lo = 20 - 500
     HVLmlo = 500 - 3k
     HVLmed = 3k - 10k
     HVLmhi = 10k - 30k
     HVL_hi = 30k - 100k
     HVLvhi = > 100k
=============================
CD4: CD4vlo = 0 - 50
     CD4_lo = 50 - 100
     CD4mlo = 100 - 200
     CD4mhi = 200 - 350
     CD4_hi = 350 - 500
     CD4vhi = > 500
=============================
